border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">那么，不看手机，现在几点了？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">You </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">jus</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> look</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed at your</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> clock, righ</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">?</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">你们之前刚刚看了时间，不是吗？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">It</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">'</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">n interesting idea. Now, I'll ask you to take </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">tha</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> step further wi</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">th a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> ga</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">me o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">f trust. Clo</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se your</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> eyes.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">非常有意思。接下来，我们把这个游戏更进一步。闭上眼睛。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">I realize I'm asking you </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">to </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">do tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> while you just hear</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> <span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">there</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">'</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> pickpocke</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> in the room, bu</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> close your eyes.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我意识到我刚才告诉你们我是个小偷，现在却要让你们闭眼睛，但还是请闭上。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Now, you've been watching me </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">for </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">abou</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> 30 seconds.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">到目前为止，你们观察我已经至少有</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">30</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">秒了。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Wi</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">th your</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> eyes closed, wha</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t am I</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> wearing? Make </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">your </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">bes</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> guess.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">请告诉我，我穿的什么衣服？尽力想。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now that he could see into the place it looked more private than ever. He went in very solemnly, looking about him. Everything was very quiet inside. Even the fountain which rose near the middle of the garden made only the faintest sound. The lovely smell was all round him: it was a happy place but very serious.     </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在他可以看到这地方的内部了，它比先前更显得幽寂。他环顾四周，庄严地走了进去。里面悄无声息，竖立在花园中心的那座喷泉也只发出微弱的声音。他的周围弥漫着一股香味。那是个令人愉快但十分严肃的地方。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 史蒂文，我们明天去购物，好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 为何后天不去呢？明天可是周六，我讨厌星期六买东西那么挤来挤去的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 但是周日和周六情况是一样的啊。如果你不介意的话，也可以的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 或许会好点吧。最重要的是一周工作后我可以有一天时间放松一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我明白了，那我们就后天去吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 顺便问一下，我们要去哪些商店呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我想在服装店买几件衣服，当我们要回来时，去肉店买些鸡肉。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们也去珠宝店买条水晶项链吧，我想为你买一条作为生日礼物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 谢谢你，亲爱的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Steven, shall we go shopping tomorrow?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why not go shopping the day after tomorrow? Tomorrow is Saturday. I hate all the hustle and bustle of Saturday shopping.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But Sunday is the same with Saturday. If you don't mind, that's okay.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Maybe it will be better. The most important thing is that I can have a day to relax after a week's work.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I see. We will go the day after tomorrow.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: By the way. What kind of stores do we need to go?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I want to buy some clothes in shopping store. When we're going back, go to the butcher's shop and buy some chicken.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Let's also go to the jewelry store to buy a crystal necklace. I want to buy one for you as your birthday present.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thank you, darling.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She watched aghast as his life flowed away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看着他的生命逐渐___________，她惊骇万分。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">消逝</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">哈佛大学研究人员领头的一项新研究表明，打屁股对儿童大脑发育的影响，可能与更严重的暴力虐待造成的后果类似。研究团队发现，打屁股会增强儿童大脑前额叶皮层多个区域的神经反应。大脑的这些区域会根据环境中的威胁等信号做出反应，并可能影响儿童的决策以及对局势的分析能力。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Spanking may affect a child's brain development in similar ways to more severe forms of violence, according to a new study led by Harvard researchers. The group found that children who had been spanked had a greater neural response in multiple regions of the prefrontal cortex (PFC). These areas of the brain respond to cues in the environment that tend to be consequential, such as a threat, and may affect decision-making and processing of situations.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;">each other </span></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span border-box;">鼓励</strong>彼此。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We're here to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">lift </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">up</span></em></strong> her spirits.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们是来让她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">振作精神</strong>的。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6037037" 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a show of hands</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a group of people each raising a hand to vote for or against sth 举手表决</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">perceptive </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英式发音/ pəˈseptɪv  / 美式发音/ pərˈseptɪv  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：having or showing the ability to see or understand things quickly, especially things that are not obvious</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：理解力强的；有洞察力的；思维敏捷的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：a highly perceptive comment 见地高明的评论</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was very perceptive of you to notice that. 你能注意到此事，真够敏锐的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">surveillance </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英式发音：/ sɜːˈveɪləns  / 美式发音/ sɜːrˈveɪləns  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the act of carefully watching a person suspected of a crime or a place where a crime may be committed</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：（对犯罪嫌疑人或可能发生犯罪的地方的）监视</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The police are keeping the suspects underconstant surveillance. 警方正对嫌疑人实施不间断监视。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">surveillance cameras/equipment 监视摄像机╱设备</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">perception </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英式音标：/ pəˈsepʃn / 美式音标：/pərˈsepʃn  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the way you notice things, especially with the senses</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：知觉；感知</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：our perception of reality 我们对现实的认识</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">visual perception 视觉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">attend</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ə'tend/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to give attention to what someone is saying</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">注意；倾听</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：I'm afraid I wasn't attending to what was being said.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恐怕我没注意听说了些甚么。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ironically </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ aɪˈrɒnɪkli   / 美式音标：/ aɪˈrɑːnɪkli  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：Ironically, the book she felt was her worst sold more copies than any of her others. 具有讽刺意味的是，那本书她觉得最糟糕，却比她的其他任何一本书卖得都好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He smiled ironically. 他讥讽地微微一笑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 40);box-sizing: border-box;">By <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</em> sh</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, border-box;">如果你猜对了，请举手。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ttention is wha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> steer</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s y</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">our perceptions,</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">但是注意力是能引导你的认知的东西，</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">is wha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> control</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s y</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">our reality.<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> It's the</em> ga</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">te</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">way <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to the</em> mind.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">它掌控你看到的现实，它是通往你的心灵的大门。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">If you don'</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> atten</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> to something, you can'</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> be aware o</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">如果你不注意某个东西，你就不会察觉到它。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Bu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ronically, you can atten</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> to something withou</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> being aware o</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">有意思的是，你也会在自己不察觉的情况下注意到某个东西。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">While he was thinking of all this he happened to look up through the branches towards the top of the tree. There, on a branch above his head, a wonderful bird was roosting. I say "roosting" because it seemed almost asleep; perhaps not quite. The tiniest slit of one eye was open. It was larger than an eagle, its breast saffron, its head crested with scarlet, and its tail purple.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他想着想着，不经意地拾起头，透过树枝一直看到树顶。一只神奇的鸟儿正栖息在他头上的一根树枝上。说“栖息”，是因为它似乎睡着了，但也许并没有真正睡着。一只眼睛睁开一条细得不能再细的缝隙。那只鸟比鹰还大，胸部呈橘黄色，头上的冠毛杂有猩红，尾巴是紫色的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 杰克，你看起来没有精神，昨晚没睡好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你说对了，我昨晚熬夜了，因为我在写一份报告。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 难怪，但是熬夜对健康不好，为什么不在第二天写报告呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 今天我上班的时候就要把报告交给经理了，所以时间很紧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 明白了，你现在肯定很困吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我已经习惯晚睡了，你呢，你睡得好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 是的，我很少在十二点之后睡觉，所以我每天都有充足的睡眠，而且晚睡对皮肤不好，就是我很在意的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 的确，女性总是很在意这件事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你为什么不早点睡觉呢？不仅对健康有益，还能让你工作更有效率。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我尝试过，但是总是睡不着。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Jack, you don't look refreshed. Didn't you sleep well last night?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: You're right. I stayed up late last night because I was writing a report.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: No wonder. But staying up late is bad for health. Why don't you write the report the next day?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I have to give the report to the manager when I go to work today, so the time is limited.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I got it. You must be sleepy right now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm used to sleeping late. What about you? Did you sleep well?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yeah, I seldom go to bed after twelve, so I have plenty of sleep every day and sleeping late is bad for my skin, which I care a lot about.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It's true that women always care about it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Why don't you go to bed earlier. Not only is it good for health, it also makes you more efficient at work.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I have tried, but I couldn't fall asleep.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I feel partly responsible for the problems we're in.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得应为我们遭遇的问题负____________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">部分责任</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">调研数据显示，近年来一些老字号或老品牌推出的创新产品，以及新锐、新兴的国产品牌产品，在90后和00后消费群体中均备受青睐，对“新国货”表示感兴趣的年轻人比例均占到70%以上。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Innovative products launched by old brands, as well as newly emerged national brands, are favored by Generation Y and Z and the proportion of young people interested in the "new national products" accounted for more than 70 percent of consumers, according to a report released by data service provider Aurora.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：go through the motions 做姿态；走过场；走形式</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I feel so bored at work, like I’m just <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">going through the motions</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我对工作感到很厌烦，就像是在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">敷衍</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We just need to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go through the motions</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们只需要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">走个程序</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>...so you need to just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go through the motions</span></em></strong> a bunch of times...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，很多时候，你只需要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">走一走过场。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>And most of us <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go through the motions</span></em></strong> of asking, "How are you doing?"</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们大多数人都会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例行公事</strong>地问:“你好吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 花费时间精力做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：not bother to do/doing XX  懒得做XX</strong></p><p 不麻烦了/别费事了</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">究竟是什么塑造了真正的你？</span><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;">电影将聚焦乔伊·高纳。这位中学音乐老师获得了梦寐以求的机会——在纽约最好的爵士俱乐部演奏。</span><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;">但一个小失误把他从纽约的街道带到了一个奇幻的地方“生之来处”（the Great Before）。在那里，决心要回到地球生活的乔伊认识了一个早熟的灵魂“二十二”，二十二一直找不到自己对于人类生活的兴趣。随着乔伊不断试图向二十二展示生命的精彩之处，他也将领悟一些人生终极问题的答案。</span></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’ll bet/I bet. 在口语中经常会出现，表示“我猜也是，我觉得也是，我相信”等等</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> ‘I nearly died when he told me.’ </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">I bet</span>!’ </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“他告诉我时，我差一点死掉了。”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">肯定是这样</span></em>！”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cat 在这里可不是“猫”噢~  而是表示“人，家伙”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① fat cat</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">是常用的美国俚语，形容那些有钱有势的人，可以解释为大亨、大款、阔佬，所以当别人对你说：You're <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">a fat cat</span>!<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>意思是：你真有钱；你真是个<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">大款</span></em>~</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Not every girl dreams to marry<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> a fat cat</span>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>并非每个女孩都梦想嫁个<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">大款</span></em>。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② old cat</strong> </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">可以表示“老猫”但形容人的时候是指“脾气很坏的老太婆，老女人”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">③ cool cat</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用来形容耍酷炫酷、追赶潮流的人</p></section></section><section wise to do XX) </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">做…不会有什么么坏处；做…是明智的</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cat 在这里可不是“猫”噢~  而是表示“人，家伙”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① fat cat</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">是常用的美国俚语，形容那些有钱有势的人，可以解释为大亨、大款、阔佬，所以当别人对你说：You're <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">a fat cat</span>!<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>意思是：你真有钱；你真是个<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">大款</span></em>~</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Not every girl dreams to marry<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> a fat cat</span>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>并非每个女孩都梦想嫁个<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">大款</span></em>。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② old cat</strong> </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">可以表示“老猫”但形容人的时候是指“脾气很坏的老太婆，老女人”</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">③ cool cat</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用来形容耍酷炫酷、追赶潮流的人</p></section></section><section out</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Digory was just turning to go back to the gates when he stopped to have one last look around. He got a terrible shock. He was not alone. There, only a few yards away from him, stood the Witch. She was just throwing away the core of an apple which she had eaten. The juice was darker than you would expect and had made a horrid stain round her mouth.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷转身向大门走去时，停下来最后朝四下里看了一眼。他吓了一大跳，原来不光他一个人在这儿，几步开外，站着那个女巫。她正在扔掉她吃剩的苹果核。那苹果汁的颜色比你想像的要深些，她的嘴边留下一圈令人厌恶的痕迹。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 朱莉亚，有个好消息要告诉你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 什么事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 这周我赚了好多钱，我在一周里赚的钱比我在两周里赚的还多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 确实是个好消息，你现在一周赚多少钱？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我的工资为每周600美元，但是我找了一份兼职工作来补贴收入。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 亲爱的，我知道你是个好丈夫。你不必工作那么辛苦，毕竟你的健康才是最重要的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我知道，亲爱的。我必须挣下足够的钱买车。我做兼职工作是为了增加收入。不用担心，我会照顾好我自己的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我明白，一定要多休息啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Julia, I have good news for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What's up?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I have earned a lot of money this week more than I do in a fortnight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It is really good news. How much do you earn a week now?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: My wages are six hundred dollars a week, but I find a part-time job to supplement my income.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Darling, I know you're a good husband. You don't have to work so hard, after all your health is most important.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I know, darling. I must earn enough money to buy a car. I do a part-time job to increase my income. Don't worry, I will take care of myself.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I see. You must have more rest.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Will you please sum up the main ideas of this article?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请把这篇文章的大意_________一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">归纳</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">调查发现，出生于80年代前的消费者喜欢购买和使用国货；从80年代到90年代出生的人群，在成长过程中明显受到欧美和日韩潮流文化的影响，因此80后和90后对于国货的购买偏好度相对较低。而伴随着国内消费市场的升级以及国民文化自信的增强，00后消费群体对于国货的购买偏好度有了较明显的提升。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">While older generations prefer to buy and use national products, those born in the 80s and 90s are less likely to purchase them because they are more influenced by the trendy culture from Europe, America, Japan and Korea. Meanwhile, Generation Z is more willing to buy national products due to market upgrading and improved cultural confidence.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cr</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ftsman /ˈkr</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ɑː</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ftsmən $ ˈk</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ræ</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fts-/ 英美元音有差异；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. tool /t</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">u:l</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">/ 注意元音和词尾舌侧音。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. craftsman n. 工匠；手艺人；工艺师</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">复数 craftsmen /-mən/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">craft n. 手艺；工艺；技能</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the writer's <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">craft</span></strong></em> 写作<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">技巧</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">craft v. 手工精心制作</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All the furniture is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">crafted</span></em></strong> from natural materials.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有的家具均采用天然材料<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">精心制作而成</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">craftsmanship n. 精工细作</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. sharpen his tools 利其器</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sharpen</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sharp adj. 锋利的；锐利的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> -en 动词后缀，表示“使具有某种特性”</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;"><li><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">darken (=make or become dark) 使变黑</p></li><li><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">strengthen (=make or become stronger) 使增强</p></li><li><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sadden （=make or become sad）使悲伤</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;">后台回复“en"，获取单词加-en后缀变动词情况详解。</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① sharpen v. （使）变得锋利 → 利</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">tools n. → 工具 → 器</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">sharpen</span></em></strong> a knife</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">把刀<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">磨快</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do I tell you how to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">sharpen</span></em></strong> your arrows?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我有指点你怎么<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">磨</strong>箭吗？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: team.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们到此<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">磨练</strong>团队技艺。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">《东城梦魇》 是由凯特文斯莱特等主演的HBO七集迷你悬疑探案剧，讲述了一个看似复杂实际并不复杂的悬疑故事。就像凯特·温丝莱特在剧中不施粉黛的真实容颜一样，《东城梦魇》这部剧本身也致力于向人们展现美国小镇不加粉饰的现实一角。</p></section></section><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.562037" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKc2x6nqDCTn6OusYk4Tr36PTryEM3O08QazppbCYh1AeFA86DUvzG8eVarzUXOLcR25O8xx2s1OHA/640?wx_fmt=png" 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">想表达支持XX，还有很多说法，比如<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">：in favour of XX; by one's side...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Be in my corner</strong>. Don't be so critical.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">站在我这一边，</strong>不要这么吹毛求疵。</p><p style="white-space:
