style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(217, 237, 244);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 5px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);transform-origin: 0px 0px;-webkit-transform-origin: 0px 0px;-moz-transform-origin: 0px 0px;-o-transform-origin: 0px 0px;border-style: none;border-width: 2px;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 10px 10px 10px 20px;background-color: rgb(102, 166, 195);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px;color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">No.9</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);padding: 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 17px;color: rgb(102, 166, 195);letter-spacing: 2px;padding: 0px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get it over with</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">赶紧结束这一些</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 0px;margin: -7px 0% 0px;transform: translate3d(12px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(12px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(12px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(12px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 13px;height: 13px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 50px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(253, 233, 164);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.562037" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKc2x6nqDCTn6OusYk4Tr36P9V209q9ZnsFv2KGDZJRLdYnWqeHuRwDc2ibBe75ZRJ3kGPQbveicu66A/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词链可以用在想让一些使自己不愉快的事赶紧结束的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Just tell me good-bye, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get it over with</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">跟我道个别吧，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">干净利落点</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Just give us our beating and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get it over with</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">打我们一顿，把这事<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">早点结了吧</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 35%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;margin: 10px 0% 0px;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 90%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKc2x6nqDCTn6OusYk4Tr36PC3caREM7xwoaBLZ2cgdhEZEqsMibUiahK8FV63CMJrKGqCdjlG7G7TIw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="258" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(270deg) scale(0.99);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(270deg) scale(0.99);-moz-transform: rotateZ(270deg) scale(0.99);-o-transform: rotateZ(270deg) scale(0.99);transform-origin: left top;-webkit-transform-origin: left top;-moz-transform-origin: left top;-o-transform-origin: left top;margin: 0px -3px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(184, 210, 237);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 7px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">TeacherGwen</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);margin: -8px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(184, 210, 237);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 0.1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">TeacherGwen</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 11px 0% 10px;text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgb(64, 64, 64);font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">口语|</strong>阅读|翻译|听写</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">编辑|排版 Claire</p></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. portion </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˈpɔːʃən/ US/ˈpɔːrʃən/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 1: a part of something larger, especially a part that is different from the other partsportion of一部分；一份</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : The main character’s childhood takes up a good portion of the film.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    主角的童年占据了整部电影的大部分内容。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 2: a particular food that is served to one person, especially in a restaurant or a shop that sells food ready to be eaten（食物的）一份，一客，一人份</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Do you have any children’s portions?你们有儿童餐吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : The portions are very generous in this restaurant.这家饭店每份菜量都很足。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 3: a share of something, such as responsibility, blame, or a duty, that is divided between a small number of people承担部分责任，负责</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I accept my portion of the blame.我承担部分责任</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : The other driver must bear a portion of the blame for the accident.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">另一名司机必须为事故承担部分责任。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. 【Phrasal Verb】come down</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 1: to descend from a higher point to a lower one.从高点下降到低点。这种用法通常用于描述降水。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Come down and look at this flood in the basement! 下来看看地下室的这场洪水！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The rain was coming down so hard this morning that I got soaked.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今天早上雨下得很大，我都湿透了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 2: verb To decrease减少。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I hope house prices in this neighborhood come down so that we can actually afford one.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我希望这附近的房价能降下来，这样我们才能真正买得起。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 3: verb To be bequeathed or passed down through a line of inheritance.被遗赠或通过一系继承而传下来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Oh, that antique vase came down to me from my grandmother.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    哦，那个古董花瓶是我祖母传给我的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 4: verb To originate with or be announced or decreed by a higher authority.由上级机关发起或宣布或颁布。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I'm not happy about this decision either, but it came down from the CEO, so we have to abide by it.我对这个决定也不满意，但它来自首席执行官，所以我们必须遵守它。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 5: verb To scold or reprimand one harshly. In this usage, "down" is typically followed by "on."严厉地责骂或斥责某人。在这种用法中，“down”通常后跟“on”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : It was a mistake, so don't come down on him too hard, OK?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    那是个错误，所以不要对他太客气，好吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 6: verb To lose one's wealth or social status. 失去财富或社会地位。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : In the early 20th century, a respected woman in high society came down dramatically if she got divorced.20 世纪初，上流社会受人尊敬的女性如果离婚，就会戏剧性地垮台。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 7: verb To become ill. In this usage, "down" is typically followed by "with" and the particular illness. 变病、生病。在这种用法中，“down”通常后跟“with”和特定的疾病。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I didn't do much this weekend because I came down with a cold.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    这个周末我没有做太多事情，因为我感冒了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Our goalie came down with the flu and missed the game.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    我们的守门员感冒了，错过了比赛。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 8: verb To be dependent on something else. In this usage, the phrase is typically followed with "to."依赖于别的东西。在这种用法中，该短语通常后跟“to”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I can't make a decision about this job until I get a salary offer—my decision really comes down to that.在拿到薪水之前，我无法对这份工作做出决定——我的决定真的归结于此。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 9: verb, slang To become sober again after using drugs or alcohol.俚语 吸毒或酗酒后重新清醒。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : It was hard to get her to come down.很难使她淸醒过来。   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 10: verb, slang To happen.俚语发生。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Hey fellas, what's coming down tonight?嘿伙计们，今晚会发生什么？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 11: noun A disappointment or failure. In this usage, the phrase is typically written as one word.失望或失败。在这种用法中，短语通常写成一个词。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Not getting into my dream school was a real comedown.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没有进入我梦想中的学校是一个真正的失败。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. a little bit of 一点点</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a little、a bit、 a little bit和a little bit of区分</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a bit与a little都可作程度副词，表示"稍微、一点儿"的意思，修饰动词、形容词、比较级等，二者可以互换。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a little bit程度比a bit与a little更轻一些，后一般加形容词。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a little bit of在句中做定语，后面跟名词。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I’m a bit tired.==I’m a little tired. 我有点累。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’m a little bit tired. 我有一点点累。受累程度轻于上面的句子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. 【Phrasal Verb】come off 摘掉，掉落，最终变成，成功</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : I didn’t come off well. 结果不太理想。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 1: come off (something) to become removed from something脱离（某物）从某物上移开</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : The label had come off, so there was no way of knowing what was on the disk.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">标签已经脱落，因此无法知道磁盘上有什么。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 2: come off (something) British English to fall off something(英式英语)从某物上掉下来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : A button has come off my coat.我的大衣掉了一颗扣子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning3: (informal) if something that has been planned comes off, it happens(非正式的)发生</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Did the trip to Rome ever come off?去罗马的事最后成了吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 4: informal to be successful非正式获得成功</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g :It was a good idea, but it didn’t quite come off. 这是一个好主意，但它并没有完全实现</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">   The performance on the first night came off pretty well. 第一晚的表现相当不错。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 5: come off something to stop taking a drug that you have been taking regularly停止服用您经常服用的药物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : It wasn’t until I tried to come off the pills that I realized I was addicted.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直到我试图戒掉药片，我才意识到我上瘾了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 6: come off best/better/worst etc (British English) to be the most or least successful, or get the most or least advantages from a situation(英式英语)最成功或最不成功，或从某种情况中获得最多或最少的优势</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : As far as pensions go, it’s still women who come off worst.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">    就养老金而言，最糟糕的仍然是女性。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Meaning 7: come off it! (British English spoken) used to tell someone that you do not believe what they are saying(英式英语)用来告诉某人你不相信他们在说什么，别扯了、别胡说、住口</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g :Come off it! We don't have a chance.别胡扯了！我们没机会。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. inventory </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˈɪnvəntri/ US/ˈɪnvəntɔːri/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">物品清单；存货；存货价值；盘点，清点存货</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. buffet </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. UK/ˈbʊfeɪ/ US /bəˈfeɪ/ noun</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a meal where people serve themselves different types of food 自助餐</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a restaurant in a station, where food and drinks can be bought and eaten（车站的）餐馆，快餐部</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">        UK&amp;US/ˈbʌfɪt/ verb (of wind, rain, etc.) to hit something repeatedly and with great force（风、雨等）连续猛击，打击</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8. follow (the) directions 按照指示，按照说明去做</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9. applause </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/əˈplɔːz/ US /əˈplɒːz/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the sound of people clapping their hands repeatedly to show enjoyment or approval of something such as a performance or speech</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">掌声</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Digory guessed at once that she must have climbed in over the wall. And he began to see that there might be some sense in that last line about getting your heart's desire and getting despair along with it. For the Witch looked stronger and prouder than ever, and even, in a way, triumphant; but her face was deadly white, white as salt.    </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷马上就猜到，她是翻墙过来的。而且，他开始明白最后一行“会如愿以偿，也会丧气绝望”可能是有含义的。因为女巫看上去比以前强壮、傲慢，甚至在某种程度上更加得意扬扬，但她的脸苍白得像盐一样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你经常从餐馆打包食物回家吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不经常。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那剩饭剩菜怎么处理呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 通常就会直接倒掉。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 真是太浪费了，人们应该少点菜，这样他们就可以减少饭店饭后食物的浪费。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 为什么人们不能少点些菜呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 在餐馆里，点很多食物是一种传统。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那最好还是打包剩下的饭菜。然而很多人不愿意这样做，但如果你愿意，你可以把剩菜带回家。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 是的，也许这是减少浪费的最好办法。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 如果你需要打包剩余的食物，服务员会给你提供打包袋。但我的妻子不喜欢打包的食物，让我很困惑。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 还好吧，我妻子也是这样的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you often take the leftover food home from a restaurant?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Not very often.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What happens to the rest of the food?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It usually goes to the dump.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What an awful waste. People should have ordered fewer dishes so that they can reduce the waste of the food at the end of the meal.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why don't people order fewer dishes?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It is a tradition to order a lot of food in a restaurant.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It is better to take the leftovers home. However, many people are unwilling to do it. But if you want, you can take the leftovers home.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, maybe it is the best way to reduce the waste.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: if you want to pack the rest of the food, the waiter will provide you with a doggie bag. But my wife refuses to eat the packed food. That makes me very confused.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: That's ok. So does my wife.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's now or never, so make up your mind.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">机不可失，____________ 吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">下决心</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">数据显示，融合了古风元素的产品最能提升年轻人的购买兴趣，其中90后中感兴趣的人群占比达54.6%，00后有73.3%。而古风元素在产品上的应用不仅包括“外在”方面，如产品外观造型或包装上的图案、图腾等，还可以体现在“内在”方面，如产品的原料应用、制作工艺等。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Products that incorporate traditional Chinese elements are most likely to increase young people's interest in purchasing, with 54.6 percent of the post-90s and 73.3 percent of the post-00s consumers interested in these products. Traditional Chinese elements are not only applied in product appearance or packaging patterns, but also can be reflected in the application of raw materials, production processes, etc.</p><p left;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.  如果你这样日夜工作，迟早筋疲力竭。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.  你大早上怎么这么激情似火？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.  止痛药</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.  这考试可真费劲。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.  她高兴得满面春风。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.  我们来这儿是为了给她打气的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.  我对工作感到很厌烦，就像是在敷衍。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.  许多年轻人都懒得投票。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.  写作技巧</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.  我上大学是为了让自己的头脑更加敏锐。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: We have to keep the romance going no matter how tired we are. The only thing worse than just going through the motions is not bothering to go through the motions.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">motions 单词尾部字母s对应的发音为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A /s/  <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">B /z/</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653556463&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=f006d7cc477223b156090c996b765c30&amp;chksm=f7ebce22c09c47345256b4b0b47ee306d5188e2d806b492cba44f29d1d8bce858f7b8b89594d&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" imgdata="null" imgurl="" linktype="text" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. A craftsman who wishes to do his work well must first sharpen his tools.">5. A craftsman who wishes to do his work well must first sharpen his tools.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">work 与 first 包含的元音是否相同？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">A  相同</strong>   B 不同</p></section></section><section style="height: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width: 24px;float: left;border-bottom: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-left: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-top-color:
